I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Existing instance of a local/anonymous Class cannot be updated
When using `readerForUpdating` with an existing object, Jackson fails with:
```
Cannot deserialize Class mypackage.MyClass$1 (of type local/anonymous) as a Bean
	at com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.BeanDeserializerFactory.isPotentialBeanType(BeanDeserializerFactory.java:883)
	at com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.BeanDeserializerFactory.createBeanDeserializer(BeanDeserializerFactory.java:137)
	at com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.DeserializerCache._createDeserializer2(DeserializerCache.java:414)
	at com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.DeserializerCache._createDeserializer(DeserializerCache.java:349)
	at com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.DeserializerCache._createAndCache2(DeserializerCache.java:264)
```

**Version information**
2.10.3

**To Reproduce**
```
package mypackage;
public class MyClass {
   public static void main(int[] args) {
       Object resultObject = new Object() {
           int value;
       }
       new ObjectMapper().readerForUpdating(resultObject).readValue("{\"value\": 2}");
   }
}
```

**Expected behavior**
Since Jackson is not required to construct an instance of the anonymous class, it should be able to populate the fields on the existing object.
Investigation shows that the method 
```
public Object deserialize(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt, Object bean) throws IOException
```
in `com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.deser.BeanDeserializer` doesn't use `ValueInstantiator _valueInstantiator` field.

So can it be made optional when you're updating an existing instance? 


</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

   934	            keyDeser = ctxt.findKeyDeserializer(keyType, prop);
   935	        } else {
   936	            if (keyDeser instanceof ContextualKeyDeserializer ckd) {
   937	                keyDeser = ckd.createContextual(ctxt, prop);
   938	            }
   939	        }
   940	        ValueDeserializer<Object> deser = findContentDeserializerFromAnnotation(ctxt, mutator);
   941	        if (deser == null) {
   942	            deser = (ValueDeserializer<Object>) valueType.getValueHandler();
   943	        }
   944	        if (deser != null) {
   945	            // As per [databind#462] need to ensure we contextualize deserializer before passing it on
   946	            deser = (ValueDeserializer<Object>) ctxt.handlePrimaryContextualization(deser, prop, valueType);
   947	        }
   948	        TypeDeserializer typeDeser = (TypeDeserializer) valueType.getTypeHandler();
   949	        if (isField) {
   950	            return SettableAnyProperty.constructForMapField(ctxt,
   951	                    prop, mutator, valueType, keyDeser, deser, typeDeser);
   952	        }
   953	        if (isParameter) {
   954	            return SettableAnyProperty.constructForMapParameter(ctxt,
   955	                    prop, mutator, valueType, keyDeser, deser, typeDeser, parameterIndex);
   956	        }
   957	        return SettableAnyProperty.constructForMethod(ctxt,
   958	                prop, mutator, valueType, keyDeser, deser, typeDeser);
   959	    }
   960	
   961	    /**
   962	     * Method that will construct a regular bean property setter using
   963	     * the given setter method.
   964	     *
   965	     * @return Property constructed, if any; or null to indicate that
   966	     *   there should be no property based on given definitions.
   967	     */
   968	    protected SettableBeanProperty constructSettableProperty(DeserializationContext ctxt,
   969	            BeanDescription.Supplier beanDescRef, BeanPropertyDefinition propDef,
   970	            JavaType propType0)
   971	    {
   972	        // need to ensure method is callable (for non-public)
   973	        AnnotatedMember mutator = propDef.getNonConstructorMutator();
   974	        // 08-Sep-2016, tatu: issues like [databind#1342] suggest something fishy
   975	        //   going on; add sanity checks to try to pin down actual problem...
   976	        //   Possibly passing creator parameter?
   977	        if (mutator == null) {
   978	            ctxt.reportBadPropertyDefinition(beanDescRef, propDef, "No non-constructor mutator available");
   979	        }
   980	        JavaType type = resolveMemberAndTypeAnnotations(ctxt, mutator, propType0);
   981	        // Does the Method specify the deserializer to use? If so, let's use it.
   982	        TypeDeserializer typeDeser = (TypeDeserializer) type.getTypeHandler();
   983	        ValueDeserializer<?> deser = findDeserializerFromAnnotation(ctxt, mutator);
   984	        if (deser == null) {
   985	            deser = (ValueDeserializer<?>) type.getValueHandler();
   986	        }
   987	        SettableBeanProperty prop = new MethodProperty(propDef, type, typeDeser,
   988	                beanDescRef.getClassAnnotations(), mutator);
   989	        if (deser != null) {
   990	            deser = ctxt.handlePrimaryContextualization(deser, prop, type);
   991	            prop = prop.withValueDeserializer(deser);
   992	        }
   993	        // need to retain name of managed forward references:
   994	        AnnotationIntrospector.ReferenceProperty ref = propDef.findReferenceType();
   995	        if (ref != null && ref.isManagedReference()) {
   996	            prop.setManagedReferenceName(ref.getName());
   997	        }
   998	        ObjectIdInfo objectIdInfo = propDef.findObjectIdInfo();
   999	        if (objectIdInfo != null){
  1000	            prop.setObjectIdInfo(objectIdInfo);
  1001	        }
  1002	        return prop;
  1003	    }
  1004	
  1005	    /**
  1006	     * Method that will construct a regular bean property setter using
  1007	     * the given setter method.
  1008	     */
  1009	    protected SettableBeanProperty constructSetterlessProperty(DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1010	            BeanDescription beanDesc, BeanPropertyDefinition propDef)
  1011	    {
  1012	        final AnnotatedMethod getter = propDef.getGetter();
  1013	        JavaType type = resolveMemberAndTypeAnnotations(ctxt, getter, getter.getType());
  1014	        TypeDeserializer typeDeser = (TypeDeserializer) type.getTypeHandler();
  1015	        SettableBeanProperty prop = new SetterlessProperty(propDef, type, typeDeser,
  1016	                beanDesc.getClassAnnotations(), getter);
  1017	        ValueDeserializer<?> deser = findDeserializerFromAnnotation(ctxt, getter);
  1018	        if (deser == null) {
  1019	            deser = (ValueDeserializer<?>) type.getValueHandler();
  1020	        }
  1021	        if (deser != null) {
  1022	            deser = ctxt.handlePrimaryContextualization(deser, prop, type);
  1023	            prop = prop.withValueDeserializer(deser);
  1024	        }
  1025	        return prop;
  1026	    }
  1027	
  1028	    /*
  1029	    /**********************************************************
  1030	    /* Helper methods for Bean deserializer, other
  1031	    /**********************************************************
  1032	     */
  1033	
  1034	    /**
  1035	     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
  1036	     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
  1037	     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
  1038	     *<p>
  1039	     * Note that usually we shouldn't really be getting these sort of
  1040	     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
  1041	     */
  1042	    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
  1043	    {
  1044	        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
  1045	        if (typeStr != null) {
  1046	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
  1047	        }
  1048	        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
  1049	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Proxy class "+type.getName()+" as a Bean");
  1050	        }
  1051	        // also: can't deserialize some local classes: static are ok; in-method not;
  1052	        // other non-static inner classes are ok
  1053	        typeStr = ClassUtil.isLocalType(type, true);
  1054	        if (typeStr != null) {
  1055	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
  1056	        }
  1057	        return true;
  1058	    }
  1059	
  1060	    /**
  1061	     * Helper method that will check whether given raw type is marked as always ignorable
  1062	     * (for purpose of ignoring properties with type)
  1063	     */
  1064	    protected boolean isIgnorableType(DeserializationContext ctxt, BeanPropertyDefinition propDef,
  1065	            Class<?> type, Map<Class<?>,Boolean> ignoredTypes)
  1066	    {
  1067	        Boolean status = ignoredTypes.get(type);
  1068	        if (status != null) {
  1069	            return status.booleanValue();
  1070	        }
  1071	        // 22-Oct-2016, tatu: Slight check to skip primitives, String
  1072	        if ((type == String.class) || type.isPrimitive()) {
  1073	            status = Boolean.FALSE;
  1074	        } else {
  1075	            // 21-Apr-2016, tatu: For 2.8, can specify config overrides
  1076	            final DeserializationConfig config = ctxt.getConfig();
  1077	            status = config.getConfigOverride(type).getIsIgnoredType();
  1078	            if (status == null) {
  1079	                AnnotatedClass classAnnotations = ctxt.introspectClassAnnotations(type);
  1080	                status = ctxt.getAnnotationIntrospector().isIgnorableType(config, classAnnotations);
  1081	                // We default to 'false', i.e. not ignorable
  1082	                if (status == null) {
  1083	                    status = Boolean.FALSE;
  1084	                }
  1085	            }
  1086	        }
  1087	        ignoredTypes.put(type, status);
  1088	        return status.booleanValue();
  1089	    }
  1090	
  1091	    protected void _validateSubType(DeserializationContext ctxt, JavaType type,
  1092	            BeanDescription.Supplier beanDescRef)
  1093	    {
  1094	        SubTypeValidator.instance().validateSubType(ctxt, type, beanDescRef);
  1095	    }
  1096	
  1097	    /**
  1098	     * Helper method for constructing back-reference property when using Builder pattern.
  1099	     *
  1100	     * @since 3.1
  1101	     */
  1102	    protected SettableBeanProperty constructBuilderBackRefProperty(DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1103	            JavaType builtType, BeanPropertyDefinition builderRefProp)
  1104	    {
  1105	        BeanDescription.Supplier targetDescRef = ctxt.lazyIntrospectBeanDescription(builtType);
  1106	        BeanDescription targetDesc = targetDescRef.get();
  1107	
  1108	        // find back reference with same field
  1109	        String propName = builderRefProp.getName();
  1110	        for (BeanPropertyDefinition propDef : targetDesc.findProperties()) {
  1111	            if (propName.equals(propDef.getName()) && propDef.hasField()) {
  1112	                AnnotatedField field = propDef.getField();
  1113	                JavaType propertyType = field.getType();
  1114	                return constructSettableProperty(ctxt, targetDescRef, propDef, propertyType);
  1115	            }
  1116	        }
  1117	
  1118	        return null;
  1119	    }
  1120	}

  1155	        tokens.writeEndObject();
  1156	        _unwrappedPropertyHandler.processUnwrapped(p, ctxt, bean, tokens, hasUnwrappedContent);
  1157	        return bean;
  1158	    }
  1159	
  1160	    @SuppressWarnings("resource")
  1161	    protected Object deserializeUsingPropertyBasedWithUnwrapped(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt)
  1162	        throws JacksonException
  1163	    {
  1164	        // 01-Dec-2016, tatu: Note: This IS legal to call, but only when unwrapped
  1165	        //    value itself is NOT passed via `CreatorProperty` (which isn't supported).
  1166	        //    Ok however to pass via setter or field.
  1167	
  1168	        final PropertyBasedCreator creator = _propertyBasedCreator;
  1169	        PropertyValueBuffer buffer = creator.startBuilding(p, ctxt, _objectIdReader);
  1170	
  1171	        TokenBuffer tokens = ctxt.bufferForInputBuffering(p);
  1172	        tokens.writeStartObject();
  1173	
  1174	        final boolean isRecord = _beanType.isRecordType();
  1175	        boolean hasUnwrappedContent = false;
  1176	        JsonToken t = p.currentToken();
  1177	        for (; t == JsonToken.PROPERTY_NAME; t = p.nextToken()) {
  1178	            String propName = p.currentName();
  1179	            p.nextToken(); // to point to value
  1180	            // creator property?
  1181	            final SettableBeanProperty creatorProp = creator.findCreatorProperty(propName);
  1182	            // Object Id property?
  1183	            if (buffer.readIdProperty(propName) && creatorProp == null) {
  1184	                continue;
  1185	            }
  1186	
  1187	            if (creatorProp != null) {
  1188	                // [databind#1381]: if useInput=FALSE, skip deserialization from input
  1189	                if (creatorProp.isInjectionOnly()) {
  1190	                    // Skip the input value, will be injected later in PropertyValueBuffer
  1191	                    p.skipChildren();
  1192	                    continue;
  1193	                }
  1194	                // [databind#4629] Need to check for ignored properties for Creator properties since
  1195	                // Records will have a valid 'creatorProp', so if we don't
  1196	                // check for ignore first, the ignore configuration will be bypassed.
  1197	                if (isRecord && IgnorePropertiesUtil.shouldIgnore(propName, _ignorableProps, _includableProps)) {
  1198	                    handleIgnoredProperty(p, ctxt, handledType(), propName);
  1199	                    continue;
  1200	                }
  1201	                // Last creator property to set?
  1202	                // [databind#4690] cannot quit early as optimization any more
  1203	                // if (buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp, value)) { ... build ... }
  1204	                buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp,
  1205	                        _deserializeWithErrorWrapping(p, ctxt, creatorProp));
  1206	
  1207	                continue;
  1208	            }
  1209	            // regular property? needs buffering
  1210	            int ix = _propNameMatcher.matchName(propName);
  1211	            if (ix >= 0) {
  1212	                SettableBeanProperty prop = _propsByIndex[ix];
  1213	                buffer.bufferProperty(prop, _deserializeWithErrorWrapping(p, ctxt, prop));
  1214	                continue;
  1215	            }
  1216	            // 29-Nov-2016, tatu: probably should try to avoid sending content
  1217	            //    both to any setter AND buffer... but, for now, the only thing
  1218	            //    we can do.
  1219	            // 19-Dec-2025: [databind#650] We can now distinguish the cases
  1220	            // but... others should be passed to unwrapped property deserializers
  1221	            if (_unwrappedPropertyHandler.hasUnwrappedProperty(propName)) {
  1222	                hasUnwrappedContent = true;
  1223	                tokens.writeName(propName);
  1224	                tokens.copyCurrentStructure(p);
  1225	            } else if (_anySetter == null) {
  1226	                // [databind#650]: priority: @JsonIgnoreProperties > FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES
  1227	                if (_ignoreAllUnknown) {
  1228	                    p.skipChildren();
  1229	                } else if (IgnorePropertiesUtil.shouldIgnore(propName, _ignorableProps, _includableProps)) {
  1230	                    handleIgnoredProperty(p, ctxt, handledType(), propName);
  1231	                } else if (ctxt.isEnabled(DeserializationFeature.FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES)) {
  1232	                    throw UnrecognizedPropertyException.from(p, handledType(), propName, getKnownPropertyNames());
  1233	                } else {
  1234	                    p.skipChildren();
  1235	                }
  1236	            } else {
  1237	                // Need to copy to a separate buffer first
  1238	                TokenBuffer b2 = ctxt.bufferAsCopyOfValue(p);
  1239	                tokens.writeName(propName);
  1240	                tokens.append(b2);
  1241	                try {
  1242	                    buffer.bufferAnyProperty(_anySetter, propName,
  1243	                            _anySetter.deserialize(b2.asParserOnFirstToken(ctxt), ctxt));
  1244	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1245	                    throw wrapAndThrow(e, _beanType.getRawClass(), propName, ctxt);
  1246	                }
  1247	            }
  1248	        }
  1249	
  1250	        tokens.writeEndObject();
  1251	
  1252	        // We could still have some not-yet-set creator properties that are unwrapped.
  1253	        // These have to be processed last, because 'tokens' contains all properties
  1254	        // that remain after regular deserialization.
  1255	        buffer = _unwrappedPropertyHandler.processUnwrappedCreatorProperties(p, ctxt, buffer, tokens);
  1256	
  1257	        // We hit END_OBJECT, so:
  1258	        Object bean;
  1259	        try {
  1260	            bean = creator.build(ctxt, buffer);
  1261	        } catch (Exception e) {
  1262	            return wrapInstantiationProblem(ctxt, e);
  1263	        }
  1264	        p.assignCurrentValue(bean);
  1265	
  1266	        // [databind#4938] Since 2.19, allow returning `null` from creator,
  1267	        //  but if so, need to skip all possibly relevant content
  1268	        if (bean == null) {
  1269	            // no "referrings" here either:
  1270	            _handleNullFromPropsBasedCreator(p, ctxt, null, null);
  1271	            return null;
  1272	        }
  1273	        if (bean.getClass() != _beanType.getRawClass()) {
  1274	            return ctxt.reportInputMismatch(_beanType,
  1275	                    "Cannot create polymorphic instances with unwrapped values");
  1276	        }
  1277	        return _unwrappedPropertyHandler.processUnwrapped(p, ctxt, bean, tokens, hasUnwrappedContent);
  1278	    }
  1279	
  1280	    /*
  1281	    /**********************************************************************
  1282	    /* Handling for cases where we have property/-ies with external type id
  1283	    /**********************************************************************
  1284	     */
  1285	
  1286	    protected Object deserializeWithExternalTypeId(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt)
  1287	        throws JacksonException
  1288	    {
  1289	        if (_propertyBasedCreator != null) {
  1290	            return deserializeUsingPropertyBasedWithExternalTypeId(p, ctxt);
  1291	        }
  1292	        if (_delegateDeserializer != null) {
  1293	            /* 24-Nov-2015, tatu: Use of delegating creator needs to have precedence, and basically
  1294	             *   external type id handling just has to be ignored, as they would relate to target
  1295	             *   type and not delegate type. Whether this works as expected is another story, but
  1296	             *   there's no other way to really mix these conflicting features.
  1297	             */
  1298	            return _valueInstantiator.createUsingDelegate(ctxt,
  1299	                    _delegateDeserializer.deserialize(p, ctxt));
  1300	        }
  1301	
  1302	        return deserializeWithExternalTypeId(p, ctxt, _valueInstantiator.createUsingDefault(ctxt));
  1303	    }
  1304	
  1305	    protected Object deserializeWithExternalTypeId(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1306	            Object bean)
  1307	        throws JacksonException
  1308	    {
  1309	        return _deserializeWithExternalTypeId(p, ctxt, bean, _externalTypeIdHandler.start());
  1310	    }
  1311	
  1312	    protected Object _deserializeWithExternalTypeId(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1313	            Object bean, ExternalTypeHandler ext)
  1314	        throws JacksonException
  1315	    {
  1316	        final Class<?> activeView = _needViewProcesing ? ctxt.getActiveView() : null;
  1317	
  1318	        for (int ix = p.currentNameMatch(_propNameMatcher); ; ix = p.nextNameMatch(_propNameMatcher)) {
  1319	            if (ix >= 0) { // normal case
  1320	                SettableBeanProperty prop = _propsByIndex[ix];
  1321	                JsonToken t = p.nextToken();
  1322	                // [JACKSON-831]: may have property AND be used as external type id:
  1323	                // [databind#1329]: if so, and visible=false, skip setting on bean
  1324	                if (t.isScalarValue()
  1325	                        && ext.handleTypePropertyValue(p, ctxt, p.currentName(), bean)) {
  1326	                    continue;
  1327	                }
  1328	                if (activeView != null && !prop.visibleInView(activeView)) {
  1329	                    p.skipChildren();
  1330	                    continue;
  1331	                }
  1332	                try {
  1333	                    prop.deserializeAndSet(p, ctxt, bean);
  1334	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1335	                    throw wrapAndThrow(e, bean, prop.getName(), ctxt);
  1336	                }
  1337	                continue;
  1338	            }
  1339	            if (ix == PropertyNameMatcher.MATCH_END_OBJECT) {
  1340	                break;
  1341	            }
  1342	            if (ix != PropertyNameMatcher.MATCH_UNKNOWN_NAME) {
  1343	                return _handleUnexpectedWithin(p, ctxt, bean);
  1344	            }
  1345	            // ignorable things should be ignored
  1346	            final String propName = p.currentName();
  1347	            p.nextToken();
  1348	            if (IgnorePropertiesUtil.shouldIgnore(propName, _ignorableProps, _includableProps)) {
  1349	                handleIgnoredProperty(p, ctxt, bean, propName);
  1350	                continue;
  1351	            }
  1352	            // but others are likely to be part of external type id thingy...
  1353	            if (ext.handlePropertyValue(p, ctxt, propName, bean)) {
  1354	                continue;
  1355	            }
  1356	            // if not, the usual fallback handling:
  1357	            if (_anySetter != null) {
  1358	                try {
  1359	                    _anySetter.deserializeAndSet(p, ctxt, bean, propName);
  1360	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1361	                    throw wrapAndThrow(e, bean, propName, ctxt);
  1362	                }
  1363	                continue;
  1364	            }
  1365	            // Unknown: let's call handler method
  1366	            handleUnknownProperty(p, ctxt, bean, p.currentName());
  1367	        }
  1368	        // and when we get this far, let's try finalizing the deal:
  1369	        return ext.complete(p, ctxt, bean);
  1370	    }
  1371	
  1372	    @SuppressWarnings("resource")
  1373	    protected Object deserializeUsingPropertyBasedWithExternalTypeId(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt)
  1374	        throws JacksonException
  1375	    {
  1376	        final ExternalTypeHandler ext = _externalTypeIdHandler.start();
  1377	        final PropertyBasedCreator creator = _propertyBasedCreator;
  1378	        PropertyValueBuffer buffer = creator.startBuilding(p, ctxt, _objectIdReader);
  1379	
  1380	        for (JsonToken t = p.currentToken(); t == JsonToken.PROPERTY_NAME; t = p.nextToken()) {
  1381	            String propName = p.currentName();
  1382	            t = p.nextToken(); // to point to value
  1383	            // creator property?
  1384	            final SettableBeanProperty creatorProp = creator.findCreatorProperty(propName);
  1385	            // Object Id property?
  1386	            if (buffer.readIdProperty(propName) && creatorProp == null) {
  1387	                continue;
  1388	            }
  1389	            if (creatorProp != null) {
  1390	                // [databind#1381]: if useInput=FALSE, skip deserialization from input
  1391	                if (creatorProp.isInjectionOnly()) {
  1392	                    // Skip the input value, will be injected later in PropertyValueBuffer
  1393	                    p.skipChildren();
  1394	                    continue;
  1395	                }
  1396	
  1397	                // first: let's check to see if this might be part of value with external type id:
  1398	                // 11-Sep-2015, tatu: Important; do NOT pass buffer as last arg, but null,
  1399	                //   since it is not the bean
  1400	                if (!ext.handlePropertyValue(p, ctxt, propName, null)) {
  1401	                    // Last creator property to set?
  1402	                    // [databind#4690] cannot quit early as optimization any more
  1403	                    // if (buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp, value)) { ... build ... }
  1404	                    buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp,
  1405	                            _deserializeWithErrorWrapping(p, ctxt, creatorProp));
  1406	                }
  1407	                continue;
  1408	            }
  1409	            // regular property? needs buffering
  1410	            int ix = _propNameMatcher.matchName(propName);
  1411	            if (ix >= 0) {
  1412	                SettableBeanProperty prop = _propsByIndex[ix];
  1413	                // [databind#3045]: may have property AND be used as external type id:
  1414	                // [databind#1329]: if so, and visible=false, skip buffering
  1415	                if (t.isScalarValue()
  1416	                        && ext.handleTypePropertyValue(p, ctxt, propName, null)) {
  1417	                    continue;
  1418	                }
  1419	                buffer.bufferProperty(prop, prop.deserialize(p, ctxt));
  1420	                continue;
  1421	            }
  1422	            // external type id (or property that depends on it)?
  1423	            if (ext.handlePropertyValue(p, ctxt, propName, null)) {
  1424	                continue;
  1425	            }
  1426	            // Things marked as ignorable should not be passed to any setter
  1427	            if (IgnorePropertiesUtil.shouldIgnore(propName, _ignorableProps, _includableProps)) {
  1428	                handleIgnoredProperty(p, ctxt, handledType(), propName);
  1429	                continue;
  1430	            }
  1431	            // "any property"?
  1432	            if (_anySetter != null) {
  1433	                buffer.bufferAnyProperty(_anySetter, propName,
  1434	                        _anySetter.deserialize(p, ctxt));
  1435	                continue;
  1436	            }
  1437	            // Unknown: let's call handler method
  1438	            handleUnknownProperty(p, ctxt, _valueClass, propName);
  1439	        }
  1440	        // We hit END_OBJECT; resolve the pieces:
  1441	        try {
  1442	            return ext.complete(p, ctxt, buffer, creator);
  1443	        } catch (Exception e) {
  1444	            return wrapInstantiationProblem(ctxt, e);
  1445	        }
  1446	    }
  1447	
  1448	    protected void _handleNullFromPropsBasedCreator(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1449	            TokenBuffer unknown, List<BeanReferring> referrings)
  1450	    {
  1451	        if (p != null) {
  1452	            JsonToken t = p.currentToken();
  1453	            while (t == JsonToken.PROPERTY_NAME) {
  1454	                p.nextToken();
  1455	                p.skipChildren();
  1456	                t = p.nextToken();
  1457	            }
  1458	        }
  1459	        if (unknown != null) { // nope, just extra unknown stuff...
  1460	            handleUnknownProperties(ctxt, null, unknown);
  1461	        }
  1462	        if (referrings != null) {
  1463	            for (BeanReferring referring : referrings) {
  1464	               referring.setBean(null);
  1465	            }
  1466	        }
  1467	    }
  1468	
  1469	    /**
  1470	     * Method called if an unexpected token (other then {@code JsonToken.PROPERTY_NAME})
  1471	     * is found after POJO has been instantiated and partially bound.
  1472	     *
  1473	     * @since 3.0
  1474	     */
  1475	    protected Object _handleUnexpectedWithin(JsonParser p,
  1476	            DeserializationContext ctxt, Object bean) throws JacksonException
  1477	    {
  1478	        return ctxt.handleUnexpectedToken(getValueType(ctxt), p);
  1479	    }
  1480	
  1481	    static class BeanReferring extends Referring
  1482	    {
  1483	        private final DeserializationContext _context;
  1484	        private final SettableBeanProperty _prop;
  1485	        private Object _bean;
  1486	
  1487	        // [databind#3030]: Store resolved value for deferred application
  1488	        private Object _resolvedValue;
  1489	
  1490	        BeanReferring(DeserializationContext ctxt, UnresolvedForwardReference ref,
  1491	                JavaType valueType, PropertyValueBuffer buffer, SettableBeanProperty prop)
  1492	        {
  1493	            super(ref, valueType);
  1494	            _context = ctxt;
  1495	            _prop = prop;
  1496	        }
  1497	
  1498	        public void setBean(Object bean) {
  1499	            _bean = bean;
  1500	            // [databind#3030]: Apply deferred forward reference resolution
  1501	            if (_resolvedValue != null) {
  1502	                _prop.set(_context, _bean, _resolvedValue);
  1503	                _resolvedValue = null;
  1504	            }
  1505	        }
  1506	
  1507	        @Override
  1508	        public void handleResolvedForwardReference(DeserializationContext ctxt,
  1509	                Object id, Object value)
  1510	        {
  1511	            if (_bean == null) {
  1512	                // [databind#3030]: Defer: bean not yet available (e.g. due to injectable constructor params)
  1513	                _resolvedValue = value;
  1514	            } else {
  1515	                _prop.set(ctxt, _bean, value);
  1516	            }
  1517	        }
  1518	
  1519	        @Override
  1520	        public boolean refersTo(Object obj) {
  1521	            return _bean == obj;
  1522	        }
  1523	    }
  1524	}

   248	    public Object deserialize(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt, Object bean) throws JacksonException
   249	    {
   250	        // [databind#631]: Assign current value, to be accessible by custom serializers
   251	        p.assignCurrentValue(bean);
   252	        if (_injectables != null) {
   253	            injectValues(ctxt, bean);
   254	        }
   255	        // [databind#3079]: Records are immutable, need to construct a new instance
   256	        if (_beanType.isRecordType() && _propertyBasedCreator != null) {
   257	            return _deserializeRecordForUpdate(p, ctxt, bean);
   258	        }
   259	        if (_unwrappedPropertyHandler != null) {
   260	            return deserializeWithUnwrapped(p, ctxt, bean);
   261	        }
   262	        if (_externalTypeIdHandler != null) {
   263	            return deserializeWithExternalTypeId(p, ctxt, bean);
   264	        }
   265	        String propName;
   266	
   267	        // 23-Mar-2010, tatu: In some cases, we start with full JSON object too...
   268	        if (p.isExpectedStartObjectToken()) {
   269	            propName = p.nextName();
   270	            if (propName == null) {
   271	                return bean;
   272	            }
   273	        } else if (p.hasTokenId(JsonTokenId.ID_PROPERTY_NAME)) {
   274	            propName = p.currentName();
   275	        } else {
   276	            return bean;
   277	        }
   278	        if (_needViewProcesing) {
   279	            Class<?> view = ctxt.getActiveView();
   280	            if (view != null) {
   281	                return deserializeWithView(p, ctxt, bean, view);
   282	            }
   283	        }
   284	        // May or may not be interned...
   285	        int ix = _propNameMatcher.matchName(propName);
   286	        while (ix >= 0) {
   287	            p.nextToken();
   288	            SettableBeanProperty prop = _propsByIndex[ix];
   289	            try {
   290	                prop.deserializeAndSet(p, ctxt, bean);
   291	            } catch (Exception e) {
   292	                throw wrapAndThrow(e, bean, prop.getName(), ctxt);
   293	            }
   294	            ix = p.nextNameMatch(_propNameMatcher);
   295	        }
   296	        if (ix != PropertyNameMatcher.MATCH_END_OBJECT) {
   297	            if (ix == PropertyNameMatcher.MATCH_UNKNOWN_NAME) {
   298	                return _vanillaDeserializeWithUnknown(p, ctxt, bean,
   299	                        p.currentName());
   300	            }
   301	            return _handleUnexpectedWithin(p, ctxt, bean);
   302	        }
   303	        return bean;
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    /**
   307	     * Helper method for handling "update" deserialization for Record types
   308	     * (which are immutable and require constructing a new instance).
   309	     *<p>
   310	     * Pre-populates creator properties from the existing Record, then
   311	     * overrides with values from JSON input, and constructs a new Record instance.
   312	     *
   313	     * @since 3.1
   314	     */
   315	    protected Object _deserializeRecordForUpdate(JsonParser p,
   316	            DeserializationContext ctxt, Object existingRecord)
   317	        throws JacksonException
   318	    {
   319	        final PropertyBasedCreator creator = _propertyBasedCreator;
   320	        PropertyValueBuffer buffer = (_anySetter != null)
   321	            ? creator.startBuildingWithAnySetter(p, ctxt, _objectIdReader, _anySetter)
   322	            : creator.startBuilding(p, ctxt, _objectIdReader);
   323	
   324	        // Step 1: Pre-populate buffer from existing Record values
   325	        final Class<?> recordClass = _beanType.getRawClass();
   326	        final RecordComponent[] components = recordClass.getRecordComponents();
   327	        for (SettableBeanProperty creatorProp : creator.properties()) {
   328	            final int creatorIndex = creatorProp.getCreatorIndex();
   329	            if (creatorIndex >= 0 && creatorIndex < components.length) {
   330	                try {
   331	                    Method accessor = components[creatorIndex].getAccessor();
   332	                    Object value = accessor.invoke(existingRecord);
   333	                    buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp, value);
   334	                } catch (Exception e) {
   335	                    throw wrapAndThrow(e, recordClass, creatorProp.getName(), ctxt);
   336	                }
   337	            }
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        // Step 2: Parse JSON input, overriding pre-populated values
   341	        String propName;
   342	        if (p.isExpectedStartObjectToken()) {
   343	            propName = p.nextName();
   344	            if (propName == null) {
   345	                // Empty object: just build from pre-populated values
   346	                return _buildRecordFromBuffer(ctxt, creator, buffer);
   347	            }
   348	        } else if (p.hasTokenId(JsonTokenId.ID_PROPERTY_NAME)) {
   349	            propName = p.currentName();
   350	        } else {
   351	            // No properties to process: build from pre-populated values
   352	            return _buildRecordFromBuffer(ctxt, creator, buffer);
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        do {
   356	            p.nextToken(); // to point to value
   357	            final SettableBeanProperty creatorProp = creator.findCreatorProperty(propName);
   358	            if (creatorProp != null) {
   359	                // Override the pre-populated value
   360	                buffer.assignParameter(creatorProp,
   361	                        _deserializeWithErrorWrapping(p, ctxt, creatorProp));
   362	                continue;
   363	            }
   364	            // Regular property? Buffer it
   365	            // 09-Feb-2026, tatu: Records really should not have non-Creator Mutators
   366	            //    so leave commented out until there's clear use case
   367	            /*
   368	            int ix = _propNameMatcher.matchName(propName);
   369	            if (ix >= 0) {
   370	                SettableBeanProperty prop = _propsByIndex[ix];
   371	                try {
   372	                    buffer.bufferProperty(prop, _deserializeWithErrorWrapping(p, ctxt, prop));
   373	                } catch (UnresolvedForwardReference reference) {
   374	                    // ignore for Records (unlikely but handle gracefully)
   375	                    p.skipChildren();
   376	                }
   377	                continue;
   378	            }
   379	            */
   380	            // "Any property"?

2026-05-30 03:01:56,286 - INFO - swea-agent-FasterXML__jackson-databind-5837 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the problem. The issue is in `BeanDeserializerFactory.createBeanDeserializer` at line 137, where `isPotentialBeanType` is called. This method throws an exception for local/anonymous classes. But when using `readerForUpdating`, Jackson doesn't need to create a new instance - it just needs to update the existing one. So the check should be bypassed in that case.

However, looking at the flow more carefully: the `createBeanDeserializer` is called when building the deserializer for a type. At that point, Jackson doesn't know whether the deserializer will be used for creating new instances or updating existing ones. The `readerForUpdating` path eventually calls the 3-argument `deserialize` method which takes an existing bean. But the deserializer creation happens before that.

Let me look at how `readerForUpdating` works:

   250	            }
   251	        } finally {

   253	        }

   255	
   256	    /**
   257	     * Method that handles actual construction (via factory) and caching (both
   258	     * intermediate and eventual)
   259	     */
   260	    protected ValueDeserializer<Object> _createAndCache2(DeserializationContext ctxt,
   261	            DeserializerFactory factory, JavaType type, boolean isCustom)
   262	    {
   263	        ValueDeserializer<Object> deser;
   264	        try {
   265	            deser = _createDeserializer(ctxt, factory, type);
   266	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException iae) {
   267	            // We better only expose checked exceptions, since those
   268	            // are what caller is expected to handle
   269	            ctxt.reportBadDefinition(type, ClassUtil.exceptionMessage(iae));
   270	            deser = null; // never gets here
   271	        }
   272	        if (deser == null) {
   273	            return null;
   274	        }
   275	        // cache resulting deserializer? always true for "plain" BeanDeserializer
   276	        // (but can be re-defined for sub-classes by using @JsonCachable!)
   277	
   278	        // 27-Mar-2015, tatu: As per [databind#735], avoid caching types with custom value desers
   279	        boolean addToCache = !isCustom && deser.isCachable();
   280	
   281	        /* we will temporarily hold on to all created deserializers (to
   282	         * handle cyclic references, and possibly reuse non-cached
   283	         * deserializers (list, map))
   284	         */
   285	        /* 07-Jun-2010, tatu: Danger: [JACKSON-296] was caused by accidental
   286	         *   resolution of a reference -- couple of ways to prevent this;
   287	         *   either not add Lists or Maps, or clear references eagerly.
   288	         *   Let's actually do both; since both seem reasonable.
   289	         */
   290	        // Need to resolve? Mostly done for bean deserializers; required for
   291	        // resolving cyclic references.
   292	        _incompleteDeserializers.put(type, deser);
   293	        try {
   294	            deser.resolve(ctxt);
   295	        } finally {
   296	            _incompleteDeserializers.remove(type);
   297	        }
   298	        if (addToCache) {
   299	            _cachedDeserializers.put(type, deser);
   300	        }
   301	        return deser;
   302	    }

   304	    /*
   305	    /**********************************************************************
   306	    /* Helper methods for actual construction of deserializers
   307	    /**********************************************************************
   308	     */
   309	
   310	    /**
   311	     * Method that does the heavy lifting of checking for per-type annotations,
   312	     * find out full type, and figure out which actual factory method
   313	     * to call.
   314	     */
   315	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   316	    protected ValueDeserializer<Object> _createDeserializer(DeserializationContext ctxt,
   317	            DeserializerFactory factory, JavaType type)
   318	    {
   319	        final DeserializationConfig config = ctxt.getConfig();
   320	
   321	        // First things first: do we need to use abstract type mapping?
   322	        if (type.isAbstract() || type.isMapLikeType() || type.isCollectionLikeType()) {
   323	            type = config.mapAbstractType(type);
   324	        }
   325	        BeanDescription.Supplier beanDescRef = ctxt.lazyIntrospectBeanDescription(type);
   326	        // Then: does type define explicit deserializer to use, with annotation(s)?
   327	        ValueDeserializer<Object> deser = findDeserializerFromAnnotation(ctxt,
   328	                beanDescRef.getClassInfo());
   329	        if (deser != null) {
   330	            return deser;
   331	        }
   332	
   333	        // If not, may have further type-modification annotations to check:
   334	        JavaType newType = modifyTypeByAnnotation(ctxt, beanDescRef.getClassInfo(), type);
   335	        if (newType != type) {
   336	            type = newType;
   337	            beanDescRef = ctxt.lazyIntrospectBeanDescription(newType);
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        // We may also have a Builder type to consider...
   341	        Class<?> builder = ctxt.getAnnotationIntrospector().findPOJOBuilder(config,
   342	                beanDescRef.getClassInfo());
   343	        if (builder != null) {
   344	            return (ValueDeserializer<Object>) factory.createBuilderBasedDeserializer(
   345	            		ctxt, type, beanDescRef, builder);
   346	        }
   347	
   348	        // Or perhaps a Converter?
   349	        Converter<Object,Object> conv = config.findDeserializationConverter(beanDescRef.getClassInfo());
   350	        if (conv != null) {
   351	            // otherwise need to do bit of introspection
   352	            JavaType delegateType = conv.getInputType(ctxt.getTypeFactory());
   353	            // One more twist, as per [databind#288]; probably need to get new BeanDesc
   354	            if (!delegateType.hasRawClass(type.getRawClass())) {
   355	                beanDescRef = ctxt.lazyIntrospectBeanDescription(delegateType);
   356	            }
   357	            // [databind#2617]: Need to apply type modifications
   358	            // (like @JsonDeserialize(as=...)) to the delegate type as well
   359	            JavaType newDelegateType = modifyTypeByAnnotation(ctxt, beanDescRef.getClassInfo(), delegateType);
   360	            if (newDelegateType != delegateType) {
   361	                delegateType = newDelegateType;
   362	                beanDescRef = ctxt.lazyIntrospectBeanDescription(delegateType);
   363	            }
   364	            return new StdConvertingDeserializer<Object>(conv, delegateType,
   365	                    _createDeserializer2(ctxt, factory, delegateType, beanDescRef));
   366	        }
   367	        // Nope, regular deserializer
   368	        return (ValueDeserializer<Object>) _createDeserializer2(ctxt, factory, type, beanDescRef);
   369	    }
   370	
   371	    protected ValueDeserializer<?> _createDeserializer2(DeserializationContext ctxt,
   372	            DeserializerFactory factory, JavaType type, BeanDescription.Supplier beanDescRef)
   373	    {
   374	        final DeserializationConfig config = ctxt.getConfig();
   375	        // If not, let's see which factory method to use
   376	
   377	        // 12-Feb-20202, tatu: Need to ensure that not only all Enum implementations get
   378	        //    there, but also `Enum` -- latter wrt [databind#2605], polymorphic usage
   379	        if (type.isEnumType()) {
   380	            return factory.createEnumDeserializer(ctxt, type, beanDescRef);
   381	        }
   382	        if (type.isContainerType()) {
   383	            if (type.isArrayType()) {
   384	                return factory.createArrayDeserializer(ctxt, (ArrayType) type, beanDescRef);
   385	            }
   386	            if (type.isMapLikeType()) {
   387	                // 11-Mar-2017, tatu: As per [databind#1554], also need to block
   388	                //    handling as Map if overridden with "as POJO" option.
   389	                // Ideally we'd determine it bit later on (to allow custom handler checks)
   390	                // but that won't work for other reasons. So do it here.
   391	                // (read: rewrite for 3.0)
   392	                JsonFormat.Value format = beanDescRef.findExpectedFormat(type.getRawClass());
   393	                if (format.getShape() != JsonFormat.Shape.POJO) {
   394	                    MapLikeType mlt = (MapLikeType) type;
   395	                    if (mlt instanceof MapType mapType) {
   396	                        return factory.createMapDeserializer(ctxt, mapType, beanDescRef);
   397	                    }
   398	                    return factory.createMapLikeDeserializer(ctxt, mlt, beanDescRef);
   399	                }
   400	            }
   401	            if (type.isCollectionLikeType()) {
   402	                // One exception is if shape is to be Shape.POJO (or, as alias, OBJECT).
   403	                // Ideally we'd determine it bit later on (to allow custom handler checks),
   404	                // but that won't work for other reasons. So do it here.
   405	                JsonFormat.Value format = beanDescRef.findExpectedFormat(type.getRawClass());
   406	                if (format.getShape() != JsonFormat.Shape.POJO) {
   407	                    CollectionLikeType clt = (CollectionLikeType) type;
   408	                    if (clt instanceof CollectionType collectionType) {
   409	                        return factory.createCollectionDeserializer(ctxt, collectionType, beanDescRef);
   410	                    }
   411	                    return factory.createCollectionLikeDeserializer(ctxt, clt, beanDescRef);
   412	                }
   413	            }
   414	        }
   415	        if (type.isReferenceType()) {
   416	            return factory.createReferenceDeserializer(ctxt, (ReferenceType) type, beanDescRef);
   417	        }
   418	        if (JsonNode.class.isAssignableFrom(type.getRawClass())) {
   419	            return factory.createTreeDeserializer(config, type, beanDescRef);
   420	        }
   421	        return factory.createBeanDeserializer(ctxt, type, beanDescRef);
   422	    }

Now let me look at the `BeanDeserializerFactory.isPotentialBeanType`:

The issue is at line 1042-1058 in `BeanDeserializerFactory.java`. The method `isPotentialBeanType` throws an exception for local/anonymous classes. This is called from `createBeanDeserializer` at line 137. 

The key insight from the PR description is:
- When using `readerForUpdating`, Jackson is not required to construct a new instance - it just needs to populate fields on an existing object
- The `deserialize(JsonParser p, DeserializationContext ctxt, Object bean)` method in `BeanDeserializer` doesn't use `_valueInstantiator` field - it just sets properties on the existing bean

So the fix should allow creating a `BeanDeserializer` for local/anonymous classes, but perhaps with a restriction: the deserializer should only be usable for updating (i.e., the 3-argument `deserialize` method that takes an existing bean), not for creating new instances.

Let me look at what happens when someone tries to deserialize a new instance of a local/anonymous class (the 2-argument `deserialize`):

2026-05-30 03:02:21,072 - INFO - swea-agent-FasterXML__jackson-databind-5837 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear picture. The `_valueInstantiator.createUsingDefault(ctxt)` is called in the 2-argument `deserialize` methods (which create new instances). But the 3-argument `deserialize` method (which takes an existing bean) does NOT use `_valueInstantiator` - it just populates the existing bean.

The problem is that `isPotentialBeanType` in `BeanDeserializerFactory` prevents the creation of the deserializer altogether for local/anonymous classes. The fix should allow creating deserializers for these types, but perhaps only when the deserializer is used for updating.

However, looking at the code flow, the deserializer creation happens before we know whether it will be used for updating or creating. So we need to modify the approach: either:

1. Make `isPotentialBeanType` allow local/anonymous types (and let the instantiation fail later if someone tries to create a new instance)
2. Or, add a mechanism to skip the check when we know we're updating

Let me see how this is handled in later versions of Jackson (since this is a known issue). Let me first look at the `ClassUtil.isLocalType` method:

   139	    public static String isLocalType(Class<?> type, boolean allowNonStatic)
   140	    {
   141	        /* As per [JACKSON-187], GAE seems to throw SecurityExceptions
   142	         * here and there... and GAE itself has a bug, too
   143	         * Bah. So we need to catch some wayward exceptions on GAE
   144	         */
   145	        try {
   146	            final boolean isStatic = Modifier.isStatic(type.getModifiers());
   147	
   148	            // one more: method locals, anonymous, are not good:
   149	            // 23-Jun-2020, tatu: [databind#2758] With JDK14+ should allow
   150	            //    local Record types, however
   151	            if (!isStatic && hasEnclosingMethod(type)) {
   152	                return "local/anonymous";
   153	            }
   154	            /* But how about non-static inner classes? Can't construct
   155	             * easily (theoretically, we could try to check if parent
   156	             * happens to be enclosing... but that gets convoluted)
   157	             */
   158	            if (!allowNonStatic) {
   159	                if (!isStatic && getEnclosingClass(type) != null) {
   160	                    return "non-static member class";
   161	                }
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	        catch (SecurityException e) { }
   165	        catch (NullPointerException e) { }
   166	        return null;
   167	    }
   168

import tools.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;

public class TestUpdate {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        // Test 1: readerForUpdating with anonymous class
        System.out.println("Test 1: readerForUpdating with anonymous class...");
        try {
            Object resultObject = new Object() {
                int value;
            };
            new ObjectMapper().readerForUpdating(resultObject).readValue("{\"value\": 2}");
            System.out.println("  SUCCESS: updated anonymous class instance");
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.out.println("  FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
            e.printStackTrace(System.out);
        }
        
        // Test 2: readerForUpdating with local class (method local)
        System.out.println("\nTest 2: readerForUpdating with local class...");
        try {
            class LocalBean {
                public int value;
            }
            LocalBean bean = new LocalBean();
            new ObjectMapper().readerForUpdating(bean).readValue("{\"value\": 3}");
            System.out.println("  SUCCESS: updated local class instance, value=" + bean.value);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.out.println("  FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
            e.printStackTrace(System.out);
        }
    }
}

I've reproduced the issue. Now let me understand the fix.

The problem is in `BeanDeserializerFactory.isPotentialBeanType()` which throws an exception for local/anonymous classes. This is called from `createBeanDeserializer()` at line 137.

The fix should be: for the case where we are updating an existing bean (readerForUpdating), we should allow local/anonymous classes. But the deserializer creation doesn't know whether it will be used for updating or creating.

The approach should be to modify `isPotentialBeanType` to allow local/anonymous types, and then rely on the fact that the `deserialize(JsonParser, DeserializationContext, Object)` method (the 3-arg one used for updating) doesn't need to instantiate. But we need to consider: what if someone tries to create a new instance (using the 2-arg `deserialize`) for a local/anonymous class? That would fail because it can't construct the instance. But that's actually fine - it would fail with a different error (from `_valueInstantiator.createUsingDefault()`), which is acceptable since you can't meaningfully create instances of anonymous classes without context.

Wait, let me look at the actual behavior more carefully. The `isPotentialBeanType` throws an exception which gets caught in `_createAndCache2`:

```java
} catch (IllegalArgumentException iae) {
    ctxt.reportBadDefinition(type, ClassUtil.exceptionMessage(iae));
    deser = null; // never gets here
}
```

So it's caught and re-thrown as a different exception. 

Looking at the code, the simplest fix would be to change `isPotentialBeanType` to not throw for local/anonymous types. But we need to consider if there are other implications.

   200	    protected ValueInstantiator _constructDefaultValueInstantiator(DeserializationContext ctxt,
   201	            BeanDescription.Supplier beanDescRef)
   202	    {
   203	        final MapperConfig<?> config = ctxt.getConfig();
   204	        final PotentialCreators potentialCreators = beanDescRef.get().getPotentialCreators();
   205	        final ConstructorDetector ctorDetector = config.getConstructorDetector();
   206	        // need to construct suitable visibility checker:
   207	        final VisibilityChecker vchecker = config.getDefaultVisibilityChecker(beanDescRef.getBeanClass(),
   208	                beanDescRef.getClassInfo());
   209	
   210	        final CreatorCollector creators = new CreatorCollector(config, beanDescRef.getType());
   211	
   212	        // 21-May-2024, tatu: [databind#4515] Rewritten to use PotentialCreators
   213	        if (potentialCreators.hasPropertiesBased()) {
   214	            PotentialCreator primaryPropsBased = potentialCreators.propertiesBased;
   215	
   216	            // 12-Nov-2024, tatu: [databind#4777] We may have collected a 0-args Factory
   217	            //   method; and if so, may need to "pull it out" as default creator
   218	            if (primaryPropsBased.paramCount() == 0) {
   219	                creators.setDefaultCreator(primaryPropsBased.creator());
   220	            } else {
   221	                // Start by assigning the primary (and only) properties-based creator
   222	                _addSelectedPropertiesBasedCreator(ctxt, beanDescRef, creators,
   223	                        CreatorCandidate.construct(config,
   224	                                primaryPropsBased.creator(), primaryPropsBased.propertyDefs()));
   225	            }
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        // Continue with explicitly annotated delegating Creators
   229	        boolean hasExplicitDelegating = _addExplicitDelegatingCreators(ctxt,
   230	                beanDescRef, creators,
   231	                potentialCreators.getExplicitDelegating());
   232	
   233	        // constructors only usable on concrete types:
   234	        if (beanDescRef.getType().isConcrete()) {
   235	            // 25-Jan-2017, tatu: As per [databind#1501], [databind#1502], [databind#1503], best
   236	            //     for now to skip attempts at using anything but no-args constructor (see
   237	            //     `InnerClassProperty` construction for that)
   238	            final boolean isNonStaticInnerClass = beanDescRef.get().isNonStaticInnerClass();
   239	            if (isNonStaticInnerClass) {
   240	                // TODO: look for `@JsonCreator` annotated ones, throw explicit exception?
   241	            } else {
   242	                // First things first: the "default constructor" (zero-arg
   243	                // constructor; whether implicit or explicit) is NOT included
   244	                // in list of constructors, so needs to be handled separately.
   245	                // However, we may have added one for 0-args Factory method earlier, so:
   246	                if (!creators.hasDefaultCreator()) {
   247	                    AnnotatedConstructor defaultCtor = beanDescRef.get().findDefaultConstructor();
   248	                    if (defaultCtor != null) {
   249	                        creators.setDefaultCreator(defaultCtor);
   250	                    }
   251	                }
   252	
   253	                // 18-Sep-2020, tatu: Although by default implicit introspection is allowed, 2.12
   254	                //   has settings to prevent that either generally, or at least for JDK types
   255	                final boolean findImplicit = ctorDetector.shouldIntrospectImplicitConstructors(beanDescRef.getBeanClass());
   256	                if (findImplicit) {
   257	                    _addImplicitDelegatingConstructors(ctxt, beanDescRef, vchecker,
   258	                            creators,
   259	                            potentialCreators.getImplicitDelegatingConstructors());
   260	                }
   261	            }
   262	        }
   263	        if (!hasExplicitDelegating) {
   264	            _addImplicitDelegatingFactories(ctxt, vchecker,
   265	                    creators,
   266	                    potentialCreators.getImplicitDelegatingFactories());
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        return creators.constructValueInstantiator(ctxt);
   270	    }

2026-05-30 03:05:46,578 - INFO - swea-agent-FasterXML__jackson-databind-5837 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand better. For regular classes, a default constructor is found and used. For anonymous classes, there's no accessible constructor. But the key point is: when updating, we don't need to instantiate.

The fix should be in `BeanDeserializerFactory.isPotentialBeanType`. We should remove the `isLocalType` check (or make it not throw an exception). Let me look at what happens if we simply remove that check - would there be a later failure when trying to create instances?

The critical path is:
1. `createBeanDeserializer` calls `isPotentialBeanType` which throws for local/anonymous types
2. If we remove that check, a `BeanDeserializer` would be created
3. For the update path (3-arg `deserialize`), it would work fine since no instantiation is needed
4. For the creation path (2-arg `deserialize`), it would call `_valueInstantiator.createUsingDefault(ctxt)` which would likely fail because anonymous classes don't have accessible constructors - but it would be a different error, and that's actually acceptable

However, we should also consider: what if the class is abstract? The `isPotentialBeanType` already checks that via `canBeABeanType`. And the `isLocalType` check also returns "local/anonymous" for non-static method-local classes. For anonymous classes, `createUsingDefault` would fail because there's no no-arg constructor available. For method-local classes (non-anonymous), they might actually have a default constructor and could potentially be instantiated - but that's fine, they should be allowed.

Let me look at the actual fix. The PR description says:
> Since Jackson is not required to construct an instance of the anonymous class, it should be able to populate the fields on the existing object.

So the fix should allow creating deserializers for local/anonymous types, and let the instantiation fail naturally if someone tries to create a new instance (which would be a different error path).

Let me implement the fix

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/src/main/java/tools/jackson/databind/deser/BeanDeserializerFactory.java   --old_str '/**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn'"'"'t really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Proxy class "+type.getName()+" as a Bean");
        }
        // also: can'"'"'t deserialize some local classes: static are ok; in-method not;
        // other non-static inner classes are ok
        typeStr = ClassUtil.isLocalType(type, true);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        return true;
    }' --new_str '/**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn'"'"'t really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     *<p>
     * NOTE: as per [databind#XXX] we can allow local/anonymous types
     * here since {@code readerForUpdating} can be used to update existing
     * instances of such types (without constructing new instances).
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Proxy class "+type.getName()+" as a Bean");
        }
        return true;
    }'

    /**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn't really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Proxy class "+type.getName()+" as a Bean");

        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        return true;
    }

    content = f.read()
old = '''    /**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn't really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot deserialize Class \"+type.getName()+\" (of type \"+typeStr+\") as a Bean\");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot deserialize Proxy class \"+type.getName()+\" as a Bean\");
        }
        // also: can't deserialize some local classes: static are ok; in-method not;
        // other non-static inner classes are ok
        typeStr = ClassUtil.isLocalType(type, true);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot deserialize Class \"+type.getName()+\" (of type \"+typeStr+\") as a Bean\");
        }
        return true;
    }'''
new = '''    /**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn't really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     *<p>
     * NOTE: as per [databind#XXX] we can allow local/anonymous types
     * here since {@code readerForUpdating} can be used to update existing
     * instances of such types (without constructing new instances).
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot deserialize Class \"+type.getName()+\" (of type \"+typeStr+\") as a Bean\");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot deserialize Proxy class \"+type.getName()+\" as a Bean\");
        }
        return true;
    }'''

2026-05-30 03:08:45,938 - INFO - swea-agent-FasterXML__jackson-databind-5837 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

    /**
     * Helper method used to skip processing for types that we know
     * cannot be (i.e. are never consider to be) beans:
     * things like primitives, Arrays, Enums, and proxy types.
     *<p>
     * Note that usually we shouldn't really be getting these sort of
     * types anyway; but better safe than sorry.
     */
    protected boolean isPotentialBeanType(Class<?> type)
    {
        String typeStr = ClassUtil.canBeABeanType(type);
        if (typeStr != null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Class "+type.getName()+" (of type "+typeStr+") as a Bean");
        }
        if (ClassUtil.isProxyType(type)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cannot deserialize Proxy class "+type.getName()+" as a Bean");
        }

        return true;

import tools.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;

public class TestCreate {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        // Test: try to create new instance of anonymous class
        System.out.println("Test: Creating new instance of anonymous class...");
        try {
            Object result = new ObjectMapper().readValue("{\"value\": 2}", new Object() {
                int value;
            }.getClass());
            System.out.println("  SUCCESS: " + result);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.out.println("  FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
            // This is acceptable - anonymous classes can't be instantiated directly
        }
        
        // Test: try to create new instance of local class
        System.out.println("\nTest: Creating new instance of local class...");
        try {
            class LocalBean {
                public int value;
            }
            LocalBean bean = new ObjectMapper().readValue("{\"value\": 3}", LocalBean.class);
            System.out.println("  SUCCESS: " + bean + " value=" + bean.value);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.out.println("  FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
        }
    }
}
